          <script type="text/javascript">
           jQuery(document).ready(function(){
		jQuery('.ajax-fancybox').fancybox(
			{
			   hideOnContentClick : true,
			   width:600,
			   autoDimensions: true,
			   type : 'iframe',
			   showTitle: false,
			   scrolling: 'no',
			   onComplete: function(){
				jQuery('#fancybox-frame').load(function() { // wait for frame to load and then gets it's height
					jQuery('#fancybox-content').height(jQuery(this).contents().find('body').height()+30);
					jQuery.fancybox.resize();
				 });

			   }
			}
		);
		
		/* Quick Shop buttons */
		function quickViewButton(){
			jQuery('button.btn-quick-view').each(function(){
				var buttonWidth = jQuery(this).width();
				var imageWidth = jQuery(this).parent().width();
				jQuery(this).css('left', (imageWidth-buttonWidth)/2);
			});
		}
		quickViewButton();
		jQuery(window).resize(function(){
			quickViewButton();
		});
		
		
		/* button loader */
		jQuery('.products-grid li.item .btn-cart').on('click', function(){
			jQuery(this).parent().addClass('active');
		});
		
	});
	
	function showOptions(id){
		jQuery('#fancybox'+id).trigger('click');
	}
	function setAjaxData(data,iframe){
		if(data.status == 'ERROR'){
			alert(data.message);
		}else{
			if(jQuery('.top-cart')){
				jQuery('.top-cart').replaceWith(data.sidebar);
			}
			/* if(jQuery('.header .links')){
				jQuery('.header .links').replaceWith(data.toplink);
			} */
			jQuery.fancybox.close();
			jQuery('body').append('&lt;div class="add-to-cart-success"&gt;' + data.message +' &lt;/div&gt;');
			jQuery('#cart-overlay').show();
			jQuery('#cart-overlay').click(function(){
				jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').hide();
				jQuery('#cart-overlay').hide();
			});
			&lt;!--&lt;a href="#" class="btn-remove"&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;--&gt;
			setTimeout(function () {jQuery('.add-to-cart-success').slideUp(500);
				jQuery('body').css({'opacity':1,'position':'relative'});
				jQuery('#cart-overlay').hide();
			}, 5000);
			/*jQuery('.add-to-cart-success a.btn-remove').click(function(){
				jQuery(this).parent().slideUp(500);
				return false;
			})*/
		}
	}
	function setLocationAjax(url,id){
		
		if (url.indexOf('?') != -1) {
				url += '&amp;isAjax/1';
		} else {
			url += 'isAjax/1';
		}
	
		url = url.replace("checkout/cart","ajax/index");
		jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).show();
		try {
			jQuery.ajax( {
				url : url,
				dataType : 'json',
				success : function(data) {
				
					jQuery('#ajax_loader'+id).hide();
					jQuery('.products-grid li.item').removeClass('active');
					setAjaxData(data,false);
				}
			});
		} catch (e) {
		}
	}
          </script>
          <script>
           function quickview(id)
	{
		if((navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i)))
		{
			jQuery('.quick_'+id).show();		
		}
		else
		{
			jQuery('.quick_'+id).stop().hide().fadeIn();	
		}
	}
	function removequickview(id)
	{
		if((navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i)))
		{
			jQuery('.quick_'+id).stop().hide();	
		}
		else
		{
			jQuery('.quick_'+id).stop().fadeOut();
		}
	}
	
		if((navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i)) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i))) {
	jQuery(".disable-quick-view").each(function(){
 		jQuery(this).empty();
		
		});
	}
          </script>
          <div class="category-description std">
           A truly stylish lady knows that you can never have enough shoes, and Unique Vintage is your one-stop shop for all of your vintage-inspired footwear. The perfect shoe is that final piece that completes an outfit, and a great pair of high heels or adorable flats helps you strut with poise and confidence. Revamp your shoe closet with sexy, stylish and simply retro shoes from Unique Vintage, from summer-ready wedges to sky-high stilettos. Whatever the outfit or the occasion, Unique Vintage is sure to have the perfect pair of shoes for any frugal fashionista!
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Our selection of unique shoes includes dressy, classic pumps in a variety of colors. They feature patent leather options, feminine floral details, ladylike ankle straps and even bows, and their 4- or 5-inch heels will make your legs look a mile long. Browse retro heels in peep toes, platforms and everyones favorite Mary Jane styles to find the bombshell look thats perfect for you. Pair these formal shoes with an elegant A-line cocktail dress and youll be the life of any party.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           If youre a vintage darling searching for something a bit more casual, Unique Vintage even has ladylike sandals and wedges to meet all of your summertime shoe needs. Nautical stripe sandals are a retro-inspired favorite, while glamorous flip-flops will give you a look of old school Hollywood glam at the pool or on the beach. We also carry cute and comfy flats that pair perfectly with a swingy skirt or a pair of your trusty high-waisted pants on more laid-back days.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Creating a pin-up style retro ensemble doesnt have to cost a fortune, and Unique Vintages retro shoes are available at prices that are so low, you might actually think its the 1950s. With frequent sales, coupon codes and free shipping on all orders of $150 or more, you can fill your closet with sweet, sassy heels, wedges, flats and sandals for every occasion.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           So what are you waiting for, darling? Unique Vintages fabulous shoe selection is fit for a vintage vixen like yourself, so get shopping!

          function sendGaEventFilter(filterObj) {
	//alert('filter is: ' + jQuery(filterObj).attr('filter-name') + ', ' + jQuery(filterObj).attr('filter-value'));
	ga('send', 'event', 'Category Filter', jQuery(filterObj).attr('filter-name'), jQuery(filterObj).attr('filter-value'));
}

	jQuery('.gan-attribute dd ol').each(function(index){

      <script type="text/javascript">
       //&lt;![CDATA[

    // Handle Magento Email Fields
    Event.observe(window, 'load', function() {
        $$('input.validate-email').each(function(item) {
            item.observe('change', function(event) {
                captureEmail(item.value);
            });
        });
    });

    // Handle Popup Event
    if (document.addEventListener) {
        document.addEventListener('bronto:popup-created', function(e) {
            $$('.popup-dialog input[id*=inputs-email]').each(function(item) {
                item.observe('change', function(event) {
                    captureEmail(item.value);
                });
            });
        }, false);
    }

    // Trigger AJAX call to capture Email Address
    function captureEmail(emailAddress) {
        var targetUrl = 'http://www.unique-vintage.com/emailcapture/index/capture/';
        new Ajax.Request(targetUrl, {
            method: 'post',
            parameters: {emailAddress: emailAddress}
        });
    }
    //]]&gt;
      </script>
